### Architecture Pattern (Operational)
```
EventBridge (1 min) ‚Üí ExecutionFinderFunction
    ‚Üì (queries StatusIndex GSI)
DynamoDB (POLLING executions)
    ‚Üì (async invocation per execution)
ExecutionPollerFunction (parallel)
    ‚Üì (queries DRS API)
AWS DRS (job status)
    ‚Üì (updates)
DynamoDB (wave/server status)
```

### Code Components

**Execution Finder Lambda** (`lambda/poller/execution_finder.py` - 369 lines)
- Queries DynamoDB StatusIndex GSI for POLLING executions
- Adaptive polling intervals (15s/30s/45s by execution phase)
- Phase detection (PENDING/STARTED/IN_PROGRESS)
- Async Lambda invocation for each execution
- Test coverage: 47 tests, 100% coverage
- Git commit: 3164b48

**Execution Poller Lambda** (`lambda/poller/execution_poller.py` - 572 lines)
- Queries DRS API for job status (describe_jobs)
- Mode-aware completion detection (DRILL vs RECOVERY)
- Timeout handling (30-minute threshold with DRS truth)
- DynamoDB updates (waves, servers, LastPolledTime, EndTime)
- CloudWatch metrics (ActivePollingExecutions, WavesPolled)
- Test coverage: 73 tests, 96% coverage
- Git commit: c27e981, 196e789

**CloudFormation Resources** (`cfn/lambda-stack.yaml`)
- ExecutionFinderFunction definition with EventBridge trigger
- ExecutionPollerFunction definition with IAM permissions
- Git commit: 89a32d5

### DynamoDB State

  - Sort Key: StartTime (Number)
  - Projection: ALL

  - Execution 1: 3b379f6e-3b82-4729-b466-7b4080bea9f8
  - Execution 2: 17edfaa5-6caa-472f-aec9-1fdaaf9f08c0

### Critical Technical Details

**DRS Job Status Query Pattern:**
```python
# REQUIRED - Status is DynamoDB reserved keyword
response = dynamodb.query(
    TableName='drs-orchestration-execution-history-test',
    IndexName='StatusIndex',
    KeyConditionExpression='#status = :status',
    ExpressionAttributeNames={'#status': 'Status'},
    ExpressionAttributeValues={':status': {'S': 'POLLING'}}
)
```

**Execution Status Flow:**
- PENDING ‚Üí Initial state (execution created, not started)
- POLLING ‚Üí In progress (waves executing, polling active)
- COMPLETED ‚Üí Finished (all waves complete or timeout)

**Polling Intervals (Adaptive):**
- PENDING phase: 15 seconds
- STARTED phase: 30 seconds  
- IN_PROGRESS phase: 45 seconds

**Timeout Handling:**
- Threshold: 30 minutes (1800 seconds)
- Behavior: Query DRS for final job status (not arbitrary failure)
- Truth source: DRS API response determines final state

## Message 104: USER

Excellent! The DynamoDB query returned 3 POLLING executions with active recovery jobs. Key observations:

1. **3 Active POLLING Executions:**
   - Execution 1: `1d2e3911-836e-4790-abbc-92f67008518f` - has 6 servers in LAUNCHING status with RecoveryJobIds
   - Execution 2: `e9211dfe-5777-4367-bec8-14067b72f4e1` - has servers in FAILED status (ConflictException)
   - Execution 3: `ee8da9cc-c284-45a6-a7f9-cf0df80d12f2` - has servers in FAILED status (ConflictException)

2. **All have LastPolledTime: 1764363630** (about ~19 minutes ago - 16:00:30 PM)

3. **Recovery Job IDs present** - These are real DRS jobs that can be queried:
   - drsjob-309e3e6b51f5949e1
   - drsjob-36f5de7a887392325
   - drsjob-30e417ec4cb208b86
   - drsjob-33cee42b7c1d4894e

- Skipped executions (not yet time): all 3 executions

1. **Test Data Only**

   - Cannot verify actual DRS API queries until live data available

2. **No Completion Testing**
   - Test executions remain in POLLING status indefinitely
   - Cannot verify execution completion workflow
   - **Mitigation**: Unit tests cover completion detection logic
